SELECT 
    ->     date_format(FROM_UNIXTIME(tran_header_cube.tran_date), '%Y-%m-%d %H:% 
i:%s') as Request_Date,
    ->     date_format(FROM_UNIXTIME(tran_header_cube.tran_date), '%Y-%m-%d %H:%i:%s 
') as Response_Date,
    ->     date_format(FROM_UNIXTIME(tran_header_cube.tran_date), '%Y-%m-%d %H:% 
i:%s') as trans_date,
    ->     CONCAT(tran_header_cube.series,tran_header_cube.folio_number) as Seri 
es_Folio,
    ->     csy_mbrc_cube.mbrc_name as Branch,
    ->     tran_header_cube.clerk_id as Agent,
    ->     tran_line_cube.line_description as Transaction_Type,
    ->     tran_line_cube.total_selling as Amount,
    ->     tran_line_cube.id as TransactionID,
    ->     tran_header_cube.client_id as RMS_C1_ACCOUNT_NO,
    ->     "Success" as Sataus,
    ->     0 as Response_Code,
    ->     "Success" as Response_Text,
    ->     IF(tran_header_cube.void_status = 'V', 'VOID', 'APPLIED') AS Void_Sta 
tus
    -> FROM tran_header_cube
    -> JOIN dealers on dealers.dealer_tag = tran_header_cube.dealer_tag
    -> JOIN csy_mbrc_cube on csy_mbrc_cube.mbrc_branch = tran_header_cube.branch 
_id AND csy_mbrc_cube.dealer_tag = tran_header_cube.dealer_tag
    -> JOIN csy_acl_cube on csy_acl_cube.clerk =  tran_header_cube.clerk_id AND  
csy_acl_cube.dealer_tag =  tran_header_cube.dealer_tag
    -> JOIN tran_line_cube on tran_header_cube.id = tran_line_cube.tran_header_i 
d AND tran_header_cube.dealer_tag = tran_line_cube.dealer_tag 
    -> JOIN tran_line_item_cube on tran_line_cube.id = tran_line_item_cube.tran_ 
line_id AND tran_line_cube.dealer_tag = tran_line_item_cube.dealer_tag
    -> WHERE 
    ->     CASE 1 # Transaction filter        
    ->         WHEN 2 THEN tran_line_cube.line_description like '%TOPUP%'
    ->         WHEN 3 THEN tran_line_cube.line_description like '%BP%'
    ->         ELSE  (tran_line_cube.line_description like '%TOPUP%' or tran_lin 
e_cube.line_description like '%BP%')
    ->     END  
    ->     AND date(from_unixtime(tran_header_cube.tran_date))  BETWEEN CURDATE( 
) - INTERVAL 3 DAY AND CURDATE()
    -> ORDER BY
    ->   tran_line_cube.id;
